structured-concept:
block.U+1F00|7936|ἀ..U+1FFF|8191|῿
Greek-Extended (U+1F00..U+1FFF)

concept-created: {2018-07-01}

description of U+1F00..U+1FFF

description::
· Unicode-block-name= Greek-Extended
· range= U+1F00|7936|ἀ..U+1FFF|8191|῿
· plane= plane.0
· quantity-of-code-points= 256
· quantity-of-chars= 233
· script= Greek
· In this block the names "WITH LINE BELOW" refer to a macron below the letter.
[https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unicode_character_property#Block]
[ftp://www.unicode.org/Public/UCD/latest/ucd/]
